177 /* Return all but the first "n" matched characters back to the input stream. */
178 #define yyless(n) \
179  do \
180  { \
181  /* Undo effects of setting up yytext. */ \
182  int yyless_macro_arg = (n); \
183  YY_LESS_LINENO(yyless_macro_arg);\
184  *yy_cp = (yy_hold_char); \
185  YY_RESTORE_YY_MORE_OFFSET \
186  (yy_c_buf_p) = yy_cp = yy_bp + yyless_macro_arg - YY_MORE_ADJ; \
187  YY_DO_BEFORE_ACTION; /* set up yytext again */ \
188  } \
189  while ( 0 )

192 #ifndef YY_STRUCT_YY_BUFFER_STATE
193 #define YY_STRUCT_YY_BUFFER_STATE
194 struct yy_buffer_state
195  {
196 
197  std::streambuf* yy_input_file;
198 
199  char *yy_ch_buf; /* input buffer */
200  char *yy_buf_pos; /* current position in input buffer */
201 
202  /* Size of input buffer in bytes, not including room for EOB
203  * characters.
204  */
205  int yy_buf_size;
206 
207  /* Number of characters read into yy_ch_buf, not including EOB
208  * characters.
209  */
210  int yy_n_chars;
211 
212  /* Whether we "own" the buffer - i.e., we know we created it,
213  * and can realloc() it to grow it, and should free() it to
214  * delete it.
215  */
216  int yy_is_our_buffer;
217 
218  /* Whether this is an "interactive" input source; if so, and
219  * if we're using stdio for input, then we want to use getc()
220  * instead of fread(), to make sure we stop fetching input after
221  * each newline.
222  */
223  int yy_is_interactive;
224 
225  /* Whether we're considered to be at the beginning of a line.
226  * If so, '^' rules will be active on the next match, otherwise
227  * not.
228  */
229  int yy_at_bol;
230 
231  int yy_bs_lineno;
232  int yy_bs_column;
234  /* Whether to try to fill the input buffer when we reach the
235  * end of it.
236  */
237  int yy_fill_buffer;
238 
239  int yy_buffer_status;
240 
241 #define YY_BUFFER_NEW 0
242 #define YY_BUFFER_NORMAL 1
243  /* When an EOF's been seen but there's still some text to process
244  * then we mark the buffer as YY_EOF_PENDING, to indicate that we
245  * shouldn't try reading from the input source any more. We might
246  * still have a bunch of tokens to match, though, because of
247  * possible backing-up.
248  *
249  * When we actually see the EOF, we change the status to "new"
250  * (via yyrestart()), so that the user can continue scanning by
251  * just pointing yyin at a new input file.
252  */
253 #define YY_BUFFER_EOF_PENDING 2
254 
255  };
256 #endif /* !YY_STRUCT_YY_BUFFER_STATE */

258 /* We provide macros for accessing buffer states in case in the

3617  }
3618  break;
3619  }
3620 
3621  default:
3622  YY_FATAL_ERROR(
3623  "fatal flex scanner internal error--no action found" );
3624  } /* end of action switch */
3625  } /* end of scanning one token */
3626  } /* end of user's declarations */
3627 } /* end of yylex */

3714 #ifdef YY_INTERACTIVE
3715 int yyFlexLexer::LexerInput( char* buf, int /* max_size */ )
3716 #else
3717 int yyFlexLexer::LexerInput( char* buf, int max_size )
3718 #endif
3719 {
3720  if ( yyin.eof() || yyin.fail() )
3721  return 0;
3722

3725 
3726  if ( yyin.eof() )
3727  return 0;
3728 
3729  if ( yyin.bad() )
3730  return -1;
3731 
3732  return 1;
3733 
3734 #else
3735  (void) yyin.read( buf, max_size );
3736 
3737  if ( yyin.bad() )
3738  return -1;
3739  else
3740  return yyin.gcount();
3741 #endif

3749 /* yy_get_next_buffer - try to read in a new buffer
3750  *
3751  * Returns a code representing an action:
3752  * EOB_ACT_LAST_MATCH -
3753  * EOB_ACT_CONTINUE_SCAN - continue scanning from current position
3754  * EOB_ACT_END_OF_FILE - end of file
3755  */
3756 int yyFlexLexer::yy_get_next_buffer()
3757 {
3758  char *dest = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf;
3759  char *source = (yytext_ptr);
3760  int number_to_move, i;
3761  int ret_val;
3762 
3763  if ( (yy_c_buf_p) > &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[(yy_n_chars) + 1] )
3764  YY_FATAL_ERROR(
3765  "fatal flex scanner internal error--end of buffer missed" );
3766 
3767  if ( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_fill_buffer == 0 )
3768  { /* Don't try to fill the buffer, so this is an EOF. */
3769  if ( (yy_c_buf_p) - (yytext_ptr) - YY_MORE_ADJ == 1 )
3770  {
3771  /* We matched a single character, the EOB, so
3772  * treat this as a final EOF.
3773  */
3774  return EOB_ACT_END_OF_FILE;
3775  }
3776 
3777  else
3778  {
3779  /* We matched some text prior to the EOB, first
3780  * process it.
3781  */
3782  return EOB_ACT_LAST_MATCH;
3783  }
3784  }
3785 
3786  /* Try to read more data. */
3787 
3788  /* First move last chars to start of buffer. */
3789  number_to_move = (int) ((yy_c_buf_p) - (yytext_ptr) - 1);
3790 
3791  for ( i = 0; i < number_to_move; ++i )
3792  *(dest++) = *(source++);
3793 
3794  if ( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buffer_status == YY_BUFFER_EOF_PENDING )
3795  /* don't do the read, it's not guaranteed to return an EOF,
3796  * just force an EOF
3797  */
3798  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars = (yy_n_chars) = 0;
3799 
3800  else
3801  {
3802  int num_to_read =
3803  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size - number_to_move - 1;
3804 
3805  while ( num_to_read <= 0 )
3806  { /* Not enough room in the buffer - grow it. */
3807 
3808  /* just a shorter name for the current buffer */
3809  YY_BUFFER_STATE b = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE;
3810 
3811  int yy_c_buf_p_offset =
3812  (int) ((yy_c_buf_p) - b->yy_ch_buf);
3813 
3814  if ( b->yy_is_our_buffer )
3815  {
3816  int new_size = b->yy_buf_size * 2;
3817 
3818  if ( new_size <= 0 )
3819  b->yy_buf_size += b->yy_buf_size / 8;
3820  else
3821  b->yy_buf_size *= 2;
3822 
3823  b->yy_ch_buf = (char *)
3824  /* Include room in for 2 EOB chars. */
3825  yyrealloc( (void *) b->yy_ch_buf,
3826  (yy_size_t) (b->yy_buf_size + 2) );
3827  }
3828  else
3829  /* Can't grow it, we don't own it. */
3830  b->yy_ch_buf = NULL;
3831 
3832  if ( ! b->yy_ch_buf )
3833  YY_FATAL_ERROR(
3834  "fatal error - scanner input buffer overflow" );
3835 
3836  (yy_c_buf_p) = &b->yy_ch_buf[yy_c_buf_p_offset];
3837 
3838  num_to_read = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size -
3839  number_to_move - 1;
3840 
3841  }
3842 
3843  if ( num_to_read > YY_READ_BUF_SIZE )
3844  num_to_read = YY_READ_BUF_SIZE;
3845 
3846  /* Read in more data. */
3847  YY_INPUT( (&YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[number_to_move]),
3848  (yy_n_chars), num_to_read );
3849 
3850  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars = (yy_n_chars);
3851  }
3852 
3853  if ( (yy_n_chars) == 0 )
3854  {
3855  if ( number_to_move == YY_MORE_ADJ )
3856  {
3857  ret_val = EOB_ACT_END_OF_FILE;
3858  yyrestart( yyin );
3859  }
3860 
3861  else
3862  {
3863  ret_val = EOB_ACT_LAST_MATCH;
3864  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buffer_status =
3865  YY_BUFFER_EOF_PENDING;
3866  }
3867  }
3868 
3869  else
3870  ret_val = EOB_ACT_CONTINUE_SCAN;
3871 
3872  if (((yy_n_chars) + number_to_move) > YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size) {
3873  /* Extend the array by 50%, plus the number we really need. */
3874  int new_size = (yy_n_chars) + number_to_move + ((yy_n_chars) >> 1);
3875  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf = (char *) yyrealloc(
3876  (void *) YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf, (yy_size_t) new_size );
3877  if ( ! YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf )
3878  YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in yy_get_next_buffer()" );
3879  /* "- 2" to take care of EOB's */
3880  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size = (int) (new_size - 2);
3881  }
3882 
3883  (yy_n_chars) += number_to_move;
3884  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[(yy_n_chars)] = YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR;
3885  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[(yy_n_chars) + 1] = YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR;
3886 
3887  (yytext_ptr) = &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[0];
3888 
3889  return ret_val;
3890 }
3891 
3892 /* yy_get_previous_state - get the state just before the EOB char was reached */
3893 
3894  yy_state_type yyFlexLexer::yy_get_previous_state()
3895 {
3896  yy_state_type yy_current_state;
3897  char *yy_cp;
3898 
3899  yy_current_state = (yy_start);
3900  yy_current_state += YY_AT_BOL();
3901 
3902  for ( yy_cp = (yytext_ptr) + YY_MORE_ADJ; yy_cp < (yy_c_buf_p); ++yy_cp )
3903  {
3904  if ( *yy_cp )
3905  {
3906  yy_current_state = yy_nxt[yy_current_state][YY_SC_TO_UI(*yy_cp)];
3907  }
3908  else
3909  yy_current_state = yy_NUL_trans[yy_current_state];
3910  if ( yy_accept[yy_current_state] )
3911  {
3912  (yy_last_accepting_state) = yy_current_state;
3913  (yy_last_accepting_cpos) = yy_cp;
3914  }
3915  }
3916 
3917  return yy_current_state;
3918 }
3919 
3920 /* yy_try_NUL_trans - try to make a transition on the NUL character
3921  *
3922  * synopsis
3923  * next_state = yy_try_NUL_trans( current_state );
3924  */
3925  yy_state_type yyFlexLexer::yy_try_NUL_trans( yy_state_type yy_current_state )
3926 {
3927  int yy_is_jam;
3928  char *yy_cp = (yy_c_buf_p);
3929 
3930  yy_current_state = yy_NUL_trans[yy_current_state];
3931  yy_is_jam = (yy_current_state == 0);
3932 
3933  if ( ! yy_is_jam )
3934  {
3935  if ( yy_accept[yy_current_state] )
3936  {
3937  (yy_last_accepting_state) = yy_current_state;
3938  (yy_last_accepting_cpos) = yy_cp;
3939  }
3940  }
3941 
3942  return yy_is_jam ? 0 : yy_current_state;
3943 }
3944 
3945 #ifndef YY_NO_UNPUT
3946  void yyFlexLexer::yyunput( int c, char* yy_bp)
3947 {
3948  char *yy_cp;
3949 
3950  yy_cp = (yy_c_buf_p);
3951 
3952  /* undo effects of setting up yytext */
3953  *yy_cp = (yy_hold_char);
3954 
3955  if ( yy_cp < YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf + 2 )
3956  { /* need to shift things up to make room */
3957  /* +2 for EOB chars. */
3958  int number_to_move = (yy_n_chars) + 2;
3959  char *dest = &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[
3960  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size + 2];
3961  char *source =
3962  &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[number_to_move];
3963 
3964  while ( source > YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf )
3965  *--dest = *--source;
3966 
3967  yy_cp += (int) (dest - source);
3968  yy_bp += (int) (dest - source);
3969  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars =
3970  (yy_n_chars) = (int) YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size;
3971 
3972  if ( yy_cp < YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf + 2 )
3973  YY_FATAL_ERROR( "flex scanner push-back overflow" );
3974  }
3975 
3976  *--yy_cp = (char) c;
3977 
3978  (yytext_ptr) = yy_bp;
3979  (yy_hold_char) = *yy_cp;
3980  (yy_c_buf_p) = yy_cp;
3981 }
3982 #endif
3983 
3984  int yyFlexLexer::yyinput()
3985 {
3986  int c;
3987 
3988  *(yy_c_buf_p) = (yy_hold_char);
3989 
3990  if ( *(yy_c_buf_p) == YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR )
3991  {
3992  /* yy_c_buf_p now points to the character we want to return.
3993  * If this occurs *before* the EOB characters, then it's a
3994  * valid NUL; if not, then we've hit the end of the buffer.
3995  */
3996  if ( (yy_c_buf_p) < &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[(yy_n_chars)] )
3997  /* This was really a NUL. */
3998  *(yy_c_buf_p) = '\0';
3999 
4000  else
4001  { /* need more input */
4002  int offset = (int) ((yy_c_buf_p) - (yytext_ptr));
4003  ++(yy_c_buf_p);
4004 
4005  switch ( yy_get_next_buffer( ) )
4006  {
4007  case EOB_ACT_LAST_MATCH:
4008  /* This happens because yy_g_n_b()
4009  * sees that we've accumulated a
4010  * token and flags that we need to
4011  * try matching the token before
4012  * proceeding. But for input(),
4013  * there's no matching to consider.
4014  * So convert the EOB_ACT_LAST_MATCH
4015  * to EOB_ACT_END_OF_FILE.
4016  */
4017 
4018  /* Reset buffer status. */
4019  yyrestart( yyin );
4020 
4021  /*FALLTHROUGH*/
4022 
4023  case EOB_ACT_END_OF_FILE:
4024  {
4025  if ( yywrap( ) )
4026  return 0;
4027 
4028  if ( ! (yy_did_buffer_switch_on_eof) )
4029  YY_NEW_FILE;
4030 #ifdef __cplusplus
4031  return yyinput();
4032 #else
4033  return input();
4034 #endif
4035  }
4036 
4037  case EOB_ACT_CONTINUE_SCAN:
4038  (yy_c_buf_p) = (yytext_ptr) + offset;
4039  break;
4040  }
4041  }
4042  }
4043 
4044  c = *(unsigned char *) (yy_c_buf_p); /* cast for 8-bit char's */
4045  *(yy_c_buf_p) = '\0'; /* preserve yytext */
4046  (yy_hold_char) = *++(yy_c_buf_p);
4047 
4048  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_at_bol = (c == '\n');
4049 
4050  return c;
4051 }
4052 
4058  void yyFlexLexer::yyrestart( std::istream& input_file )
4059 {
4060 
4061  if ( ! YY_CURRENT_BUFFER ){
4062  yyensure_buffer_stack ();
4063  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE =
4064  yy_create_buffer( yyin, YY_BUF_SIZE );
4065  }
4066 
4067  yy_init_buffer( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER, input_file );
4068  yy_load_buffer_state( );
4069 }
4070 
4076 void yyFlexLexer::yyrestart( std::istream* input_file )
4077 {
4078  if( ! input_file ) {
4079  input_file = &yyin;
4080  }
4081  yyrestart( *input_file );
4082 }
4083 
4088  void yyFlexLexer::yy_switch_to_buffer( YY_BUFFER_STATE new_buffer )
4089 {
4090 
4091  /* TODO. We should be able to replace this entire function body
4092  * with
4093  * yypop_buffer_state();
4094  * yypush_buffer_state(new_buffer);
4095  */
4096  yyensure_buffer_stack ();
4097  if ( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER == new_buffer )
4098  return;
4099 
4100  if ( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER )
4101  {
4102  /* Flush out information for old buffer. */
4103  *(yy_c_buf_p) = (yy_hold_char);
4104  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_pos = (yy_c_buf_p);
4105  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars = (yy_n_chars);
4106  }
4107 
4108  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE = new_buffer;
4109  yy_load_buffer_state( );
4110 
4111  /* We don't actually know whether we did this switch during
4112  * EOF (yywrap()) processing, but the only time this flag
4113  * is looked at is after yywrap() is called, so it's safe
4114  * to go ahead and always set it.
4115  */
4116  (yy_did_buffer_switch_on_eof) = 1;
4117 }
4118 
4119  void yyFlexLexer::yy_load_buffer_state()
4120 {
4121  (yy_n_chars) = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars;
4122  (yytext_ptr) = (yy_c_buf_p) = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_pos;
4123  yyin.rdbuf(YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_input_file);
4124  (yy_hold_char) = *(yy_c_buf_p);
4125 }
4126 
4133  YY_BUFFER_STATE yyFlexLexer::yy_create_buffer( std::istream& file, int size )
4134 {
4135  YY_BUFFER_STATE b;
4136 
4137  b = (YY_BUFFER_STATE) yyalloc( sizeof( struct yy_buffer_state ) );
4138  if ( ! b )
4139  YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in yy_create_buffer()" );
4140 
4141  b->yy_buf_size = size;
4142 
4143  /* yy_ch_buf has to be 2 characters longer than the size given because
4144  * we need to put in 2 end-of-buffer characters.
4145  */
4146  b->yy_ch_buf = (char *) yyalloc( (yy_size_t) (b->yy_buf_size + 2) );
4147  if ( ! b->yy_ch_buf )
4148  YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in yy_create_buffer()" );
4149 
4150  b->yy_is_our_buffer = 1;
4151 
4152  yy_init_buffer( b, file );
4153 
4154  return b;
4155 }

4164 {

4166 }

4172  void yyFlexLexer::yy_delete_buffer( YY_BUFFER_STATE b )
4173 {
4174 
4175  if ( ! b )
4176  return;
4177 
4178  if ( b == YY_CURRENT_BUFFER ) /* Not sure if we should pop here. */
4179  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE = (YY_BUFFER_STATE) 0;
4180 
4181  if ( b->yy_is_our_buffer )
4182  yyfree( (void *) b->yy_ch_buf );
4183 
4184  yyfree( (void *) b );
4185 }
4186 
4187 /* Initializes or reinitializes a buffer.
4188  * This function is sometimes called more than once on the same buffer,
4189  * such as during a yyrestart() or at EOF.
4190  */
4191  void yyFlexLexer::yy_init_buffer( YY_BUFFER_STATE b, std::istream& file )
4192 
4193 {
4194  int oerrno = errno;
4195 
4196  yy_flush_buffer( b );
4197 
4198  b->yy_input_file = file.rdbuf();
4199  b->yy_fill_buffer = 1;
4200 
4201  /* If b is the current buffer, then yy_init_buffer was _probably_
4202  * called from yyrestart() or through yy_get_next_buffer.
4203  * In that case, we don't want to reset the lineno or column.
4204  */
4205  if (b != YY_CURRENT_BUFFER){
4206  b->yy_bs_lineno = 1;
4207  b->yy_bs_column = 0;
4208  }
4209 
4210  b->yy_is_interactive = 0;
4211  errno = oerrno;
4212 }
4213 
4218  void yyFlexLexer::yy_flush_buffer( YY_BUFFER_STATE b )
4219 {
4220  if ( ! b )
4221  return;
4222 
4223  b->yy_n_chars = 0;
4224 
4225  /* We always need two end-of-buffer characters. The first causes
4226  * a transition to the end-of-buffer state. The second causes
4227  * a jam in that state.
4228  */
4229  b->yy_ch_buf[0] = YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR;
4230  b->yy_ch_buf[1] = YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR;
4231 
4232  b->yy_buf_pos = &b->yy_ch_buf[0];
4233 
4234  b->yy_at_bol = 1;
4235  b->yy_buffer_status = YY_BUFFER_NEW;
4236 
4237  if ( b == YY_CURRENT_BUFFER )
4238  yy_load_buffer_state( );
4239 }
4240 
4247 void yyFlexLexer::yypush_buffer_state (YY_BUFFER_STATE new_buffer)
4248 {
4249  if (new_buffer == NULL)
4250  return;
4251 
4252  yyensure_buffer_stack();
4253 
4254  /* This block is copied from yy_switch_to_buffer. */
4255  if ( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER )
4256  {
4257  /* Flush out information for old buffer. */
4258  *(yy_c_buf_p) = (yy_hold_char);
4259  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_pos = (yy_c_buf_p);
4260  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars = (yy_n_chars);
4261  }
4262 
4263  /* Only push if top exists. Otherwise, replace top. */
4264  if (YY_CURRENT_BUFFER)
4265  (yy_buffer_stack_top)++;
4266  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE = new_buffer;
4267 
4268  /* copied from yy_switch_to_buffer. */
4269  yy_load_buffer_state( );
4270  (yy_did_buffer_switch_on_eof) = 1;
4271 }

4277 void yyFlexLexer::yypop_buffer_state (void)
4278 {
4279  if (!YY_CURRENT_BUFFER)
4280  return;
4281 
4282  yy_delete_buffer(YY_CURRENT_BUFFER );
4283  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE = NULL;
4284  if ((yy_buffer_stack_top) > 0)
4285  --(yy_buffer_stack_top);
4286 
4287  if (YY_CURRENT_BUFFER) {
4288  yy_load_buffer_state( );
4289  (yy_did_buffer_switch_on_eof) = 1;
4290  }
4291 }
4292 
4293 /* Allocates the stack if it does not exist.
4294  * Guarantees space for at least one push.
4295  */
4296 void yyFlexLexer::yyensure_buffer_stack(void)
4297 {
4298  yy_size_t num_to_alloc;
4299 
4300  if (!(yy_buffer_stack)) {
4301 
4302  /* First allocation is just for 2 elements, since we don't know if this
4303  * scanner will even need a stack. We use 2 instead of 1 to avoid an
4304  * immediate realloc on the next call.
4305  */
4306  num_to_alloc = 1; /* After all that talk, this was set to 1 anyways... */
4307  (yy_buffer_stack) = (struct yy_buffer_state**)yyalloc
4308  (num_to_alloc * sizeof(struct yy_buffer_state*)
4309  );
4310  if ( ! (yy_buffer_stack) )
4311  YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in yyensure_buffer_stack()" );
4312 
4313  memset((yy_buffer_stack), 0, num_to_alloc * sizeof(struct yy_buffer_state*));
4314 
4315  (yy_buffer_stack_max) = num_to_alloc;
4316  (yy_buffer_stack_top) = 0;
4317  return;
4318  }
4319 
4320  if ((yy_buffer_stack_top) >= ((yy_buffer_stack_max)) - 1){
4321 
4322  /* Increase the buffer to prepare for a possible push. */
4323  yy_size_t grow_size = 8 /* arbitrary grow size */;
4324 
4325  num_to_alloc = (yy_buffer_stack_max) + grow_size;
4326  (yy_buffer_stack) = (struct yy_buffer_state**)yyrealloc
4327  ((yy_buffer_stack),
4328  num_to_alloc * sizeof(struct yy_buffer_state*)
4329  );
4330  if ( ! (yy_buffer_stack) )
4331  YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in yyensure_buffer_stack()" );
4332 
4333  /* zero only the new slots.*/
4334  memset((yy_buffer_stack) + (yy_buffer_stack_max), 0, grow_size * sizeof(struct yy_buffer_state*));
4335  (yy_buffer_stack_max) = num_to_alloc;
4336  }
4337 }
4338 
4339  void yyFlexLexer::yy_push_state( int _new_state )
4340 {
4341  if ( (yy_start_stack_ptr) >= (yy_start_stack_depth) )
4342  {
4343  yy_size_t new_size;
4344 
4345  (yy_start_stack_depth) += YY_START_STACK_INCR;
4346  new_size = (yy_size_t) (yy_start_stack_depth) * sizeof( int );
4347 
4348  if ( ! (yy_start_stack) )
4349  (yy_start_stack) = (int *) yyalloc( new_size );
4350 
4351  else
4352  (yy_start_stack) = (int *) yyrealloc(
4353  (void *) (yy_start_stack), new_size );
4354 
4355  if ( ! (yy_start_stack) )
4356  YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of memory expanding start-condition stack" );
4357  }
4358 
4359  (yy_start_stack)[(yy_start_stack_ptr)++] = YY_START;
4360 
4361  BEGIN(_new_state);
4362 }
4363 
4364  void yyFlexLexer::yy_pop_state()
4365 {
4366  if ( --(yy_start_stack_ptr) < 0 )
4367  YY_FATAL_ERROR( "start-condition stack underflow" );
4368 
4369  BEGIN((yy_start_stack)[(yy_start_stack_ptr)]);
4370 }
4371 
4372  int yyFlexLexer::yy_top_state()
4373 {
4374  return (yy_start_stack)[(yy_start_stack_ptr) - 1];
4375 }

4436 void *yyrealloc (void * ptr, yy_size_t size )
4437 {
4438 
4439  /* The cast to (char *) in the following accommodates both
4440  * implementations that use char* generic pointers, and those
4441  * that use void* generic pointers. It works with the latter
4442  * because both ANSI C and C++ allow castless assignment from
4443  * any pointer type to void*, and deal with argument conversions
4444  * as though doing an assignment.
4445  */
4446  return realloc(ptr, size);
4447 }

4465 label findFace(const polyMesh& mesh, const face& f)
4466 {
4467  const labelList& pFaces = mesh.pointFaces()[f[0]];
4468 
4469  forAll(pFaces, i)
4470  {
4471  label faceI = pFaces[i];
4472

4474  {
4475  return faceI;
4476  }
4477  }

4479  FatalErrorIn("findFace(const polyMesh&, const face&)")
4480  << "Cannot find a face matching " << f
4481  << exit(FatalError);
4482 
4483  return -1;
4484 }
